	return StoreString("BASE CURR", Translate(BloombergETT, true, "BLOOMBERG_CURRENCY_CODE", BASE_CRNCY));
else if(OneHasValue(BASE_CRNCY))
	return StoreString("BASE CURR", BASE_CRNCY);
else
	return StoreString("BASE CURR", "USD");
]]></expr>
          </Execute>
          <Execute displayName="TICKER DERIVED">
            <expr><![CDATA[if (OneHasValue(SECURITY_TYP) && (OneHasValue(ID_BB_SEC_NUM_DES) && StrContainsOneOf(SECURITY_TYP, "Financial commodity option")))
	return StoreString("TICKER_DERIVED", ID_BB_SEC_NUM_DES);
else
	return StoreString("TICKER_DERIVED", TICKER);

]]></expr>
          </Execute>
          <Execute displayName="TERM CURR">
            <expr><![CDATA[if (OneHasValue(CRNCY) && OneHasValue(Translate(BloombergETT, true, "BLOOMBERG_CURRENCY_CODE",CRNCY)))
	return StoreString("TERM CURR", Translate(BloombergETT, true, "BLOOMBERG_CURRENCY_CODE", CRNCY));
else if(OneHasValue(CRNCY))
	return StoreString("TERM CURR", CRNCY);
else
	return StoreString("TERM CURR", Select("", "", "select denom_curr_cde from ft_t_issu where instr_id = (select instr_id from ft_t_isid where id_ctxt_typ='TICKER' and iss_id =:1 and (end_tms is null or end_tms > sysdate))", TICKER, "", "", "", ""));]]></expr>
          </Execute>

          </Execute>
          <Execute displayName="PRC_TMS">

          </Execute>

  <Expressions>
    <Expression enabled="true" ident="KeyStreaming">
      <expr><![CDATA[if (OneHasValue(ID_BB_GLOBAL)
		&& (Strcmp(SECURITY_TYP, "CROSS") || Strcmp(SECURITY_TYP, "SPOT")))
	return ID_BB_GLOBAL;
else if (OneHasValue(ID_BB_UNIQUE))
	return ID_BB_UNIQUE;
else
	return ID_BB_COMPANY;]]></expr>
    </Expression>
    <Expression enabled="true" ident="RecordIdentifier">
      <expr><![CDATA[return Strcat(
		TICKER,
		Strcat(";",
				Strcat(";",
						Strcat(MARKET_SECTOR_DES,
								Strcat(";",
										Strcat(ERRORCODE, Strcat(";", "OUT")))))));]]></expr>
    </Expression>
    <Expression enabled="false" ident="GSDMFiltering">
      <expr><![CDATA[return "";]]></expr>
    </Expression>
    <Expression enabled="false" ident="VDSFiltering">
      <expr><![CDATA[return "";]]></expr>
    </Expression>
  </Expressions>
